\chapter{Verb dictionary} \label{verb dictionary}

\section{Single-aspect verbs} \label{single-aspect verbs}
\subsection{Verbs taking \textsc{a}-series personal prefixes, stative aspect only}
\begin{multicols}{2}

%example reformatting begins
\lexicalunitbracket{adatgowanęh} \trs{self-important}, \trs{rash}, \trs{unwise}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

\cayuga{wadatgowá:nęh} \trs{it is rash, unwise, self-important, egotistical}

\lexicalunitbracket{ahdihęh} \trs{different}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{desáhdihęh} \trs{you are different}

\lexicalunitbracket{d} \trs{standing}

\cayuga{gá:di:t} \trs{they are standing}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{joháha:t} \trs{one road}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{sga̱hǫ́hsra:t} \trs{one box, one thousand}
%example reformatting ends

\lexicalunitbracket{+dagyeˀ} \trs{standing along, continuing on}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{oyádagyeˀ} \trs{a gulley}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{gahsyádagyeˀ} \trs{a passing herd}


\lexicalunitbracket{dręniyo:} \trs{smell nice}

\cayuga{gedrę:ní:yo:} \trs{I smell nice}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀdriyo:} \trs{be a good shot}, with (\stem{{\partitive}})

\cayuga{haˀdrí:yo:} \trs{he is a good, accurate shot}

\lexicalunitbracket{gahagaęheˀ} \trs{cross-eyed}

\cayuga{egahgáęheˀ} \trs{she is cross eyed}

\lexicalunitbracket{gahgwegǫh} \trs{blind}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{dehaga̱hgwé:gǫh} \trs{he is blind}

\lexicalunitbracket{gahǫˀji:} \trs{have a black eye}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{desega̱hǫ́ˀji:} \trs{you have a black eye}

\lexicalunitbracket{geˀa:ˀ} \trs{ragged, bedraggled}

\cayuga{gegéˀa:ˀ} \trs{I am raggedy}

\lexicalunitbracket{gęhjih} \trs{old (living thing)}

\cayuga{egę́hjih} \trs{she is old, an old woman}


\lexicalunitbracket{gohgowah} \trs{royalty, queen, king}

\cayuga{(e)gohgó:wah} \trs{queen, the Queen}

\lexicalunitbracket{gǫhsdǫˀęˀod, gǫhstwęˀod} \trs{beard}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{dehagǫhstwę́ˀo:t} \trs{he has a beard}

\lexicalunitbracket{gowanęh} \trs{big, pregnant}

\cayuga{egówanęh} \trs{she is big, pregnant}

\cayuga{hagówanęh} \trs{he is big}

\lexicalunitbracket{gowanęhgowah} \trs{really big}

\cayuga{egowanęhgó:wah} \trs{she is really big}

\lexicalunitbracket{hiˀyagaęheˀ} \trs{bent over}

\cayuga{haˀhiˀyagáęheˀ} \trs{his body trunk is crooked}, \trs{he is bent over}

\lexicalunitbracket{hnęye:s} \trs{tall}

\cayuga{ehnę́:ye:s} \trs{she is tall}

\lexicalunitbracket{hnyahdod} \trs{lift one’s head}

\cayuga{ehnyáhdo:t} \trs{she has got her head up} (said of a child who is learning to lift its head by itself)

\lexicalunitbracket{hnyǫˀǫh} \trs{white}

\cayuga{ga̱hnyǫ́ˀǫh} \trs{it is white}

\lexicalunitbracket{hretgęsˀah} \trs{unattractive}

\cayuga{hahe:tgę́:sˀah} \trs{he is unattractive}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsęnowanęh} \trs{important, famous, prominent person}

\cayuga{hahsęnowá:nęh} \trs{he is an important person}, \trs{he is famous, prominent}, (literally, \trs{he has made a name for himself})

\lexicalunitbracket{hsgwaowanęˀs} \trs{well-endowed}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{dehahsgwáowanęˀs} \trs{he has big rocks} (i.e. he is well-endowed)

\lexicalunitbracket{hsgwiˀdrahe:ˀ} \trs{wrinkly}, with \stem{{\repetitive}}

\cayuga{sgahsgwíˀdra̱he:ˀ tsǫ:} \trs{you are pruny, wrinkly} \cayuga{tsǫ:} \trs{just}

\lexicalunitbracket{hshad} \trs{lie on one’s back}

\cayuga{gehsha:t} \trs{I am lying on my back}

\lexicalunitbracket{hshaǫd} \trs{tied up}

\cayuga{ge̱hsháǫt} \trs{I am tied up}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsiha:ˀ} \trs{stand in a bunch or group, congregate}

\cayuga{gáehsi̱ha:ˀ} \trs{they are standing in a group or clump}

\cayuga{ojihsǫdáhsi̱ha:ˀ} \trs{stars showing}, \trs{a group of stars}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsrǫhę:} \trs{angry, cross}

\cayuga{ehsrǫ́hę:} \trs{she is habitually cross, cantankerous}

\lexicalunitbracket{idage:ˀ} \trs{lying prostrate}

\cayuga{sidá:ge:ˀ} \trs{you are lying down, prostrate}

\lexicalunitbracket{idagrǫˀ} \trs{several things lying prostrate}

\cayuga{hadídagrǫˀ} \trs{they are lying around}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihnatę:} \trs{dry skin}

\cayuga{se̱hná:tę:, si̱hná:tę:} \trs{you have dry skin}

\lexicalunitbracket{itsgod} \trs{sitting}

\cayuga{etsgo:t} \trs{she is sitting}

\lexicalunitbracket{itsgodǫˀ} \trs{sitting} (several people or animals)

\cayuga{gadi:tsgó:dǫˀ} \trs{they are sitting}

\lexicalunitbracket{itsgwahe:ˀ} \trs{sit on something}

\cayuga{gitsgwáhe:ˀ} \trs{I am perched up on something}, \trs{I am sitting on something}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdawęnyeˀ} \trs{shit-disturber}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{deyeˀdawę́:nyeˀ} \trs{she is a shit-disturber}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdrǫ} \trs{live, dwell, be at home}

\cayuga{hadíˀdrǫˀ} \trs{they are at home}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdrǫd} \trs{live}, \trs{dwell}, \trs{be at home}, \trs{reside}, \trs{be placed}, \trs{be situated}

\cayuga{hadiˀdrǫ́:dǫˀ} \trs{how they are placed}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀgę:} \trs{light-skinned, white}

\cayuga{haˀgę:} \trs{he is light-skinned}

\lexicalunitbracket{jaǫ:} \trs{both}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{degaejáǫ:} \trs{both of them}

\lexicalunitbracket{jinah} \trs{strong, brave, male}

\cayuga{hají:nah} \trs{he is masculine, brave}, \trs{his genitals}

\lexicalunitbracket{nagreˀ} \trs{live somewhere}

\cayuga{gáenagreˀ} \trs{where they live} (an area)

\lexicalunitbracket{nahsgwes} \trs{jump far}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{dehána̱hsgwe:s} \trs{he jumps far horizontally}

\lexicalunitbracket{nahsgwesǫˀs} \trs{jump high}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{de̱hana̱hsgwé:sǫˀs} \trs{he jumps high}

\lexicalunitbracket{nai} \trs{proud, boastful}

\cayuga{enai} \trs{she is proud in a boastful manner}

\lexicalunitbracket{+negę:} \trs{side by side}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{Tayędané:gęˀ} \trs{Deseronto} (literally, \trs{firewood side-by-side})

\lexicalunitbracket{nhodǫnyǫˀ} \trs{locked up}

\cayuga{gadinhodǫ́:nyǫˀ} \trs{they are locked up}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnigǫhahsnoweˀ} \trs{be mentally quick}

\cayuga{haˀnigǫ̱hahsnó:weˀ} \trs{he is a quick thinker}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnigǫhayei} \trs{crazy, not right in the head}, with \stem{{\negative}}

\cayuga{tehaˀnigǫhayéiˀ} \trs{he is not right in the mind}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnigǫhowanęh} \trs{broad-minded, wise, thinkers}

\cayuga{snigǫhowá:nęh} \trs{you have a broad mind}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnyǫgri:} \trs{have a stuffed-up nose}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{degéˀnyǫgri:} \trs{my nose is stuffed up}

\lexicalunitbracket{rihwagwęniyoˀ} \trs{reside}, \trs{dwell}

\cayuga{grihwagwęní:yoˀ} \trs{where I reside, dwell} (literally, \trs{where I am the boss})

\lexicalunitbracket{wayęhǫhsdǫh} \trs{right-handed}

\cayuga{hawayę̱hǫ́hsdǫh} \trs{he is right-handed}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdadogę:} \trs{between people, living things}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{detniya̱ˀda:dó:gę:} \trs{between you and me}, \trs{between our bodies}

\lexicalunitbracket{yahshe:} \trs{two living things}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{de̱hadiyáhshe:} \trs{two males}, \trs{they are two}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀtgaǫˀ} \trs{active}, \trs{quick to move}

\cayuga{hayáˀtgaǫˀ} \trs{he is quick to move}, \trs{he is active, always moving around}

\lexicalunitbracket{yehwad} \trs{early riser}

\cayuga{sye̱hwa:t} \trs{you are an early riser}


\lexicalunitbracket{waihǫh} \trs{be good at something}

\cayuga{sewáihǫh} \trs{you are good at something}

\lexicalunitbracket{yahsǫh} \trs{be named}

\cayuga{hayá:sǫh} \trs{his name is}


\end{multicols}

\subsection{Verbs taking \textsc{a}-series personal prefixes, habitual aspect only}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{adagyaˀda:ˀs} \trs{be self-centred, opinionated, snobbish}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

\cayuga{hadagyˀada:s} \trs{he has a high opinion of himself, he is self-centred, he is bold}

\lexicalunitbracket{adahǫdǫhsgǫ:} \trs{be inquisitive}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{sadahǫhdǫ́hsgǫ:} \trs{you are inquisitive}

\lexicalunitbracket{adata:ˀ} \trs{be conceited, snobbish}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

\cayuga{hadá:ta:ˀ} \trs{he is conceited}

\lexicalunitbracket{adatgǫnyǫhsd} \trs{be stuck up, snobbish}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

\cayuga{wadatgǫnyǫ́hstaˀ} \trs{she (literally, it) is stuck up}

\lexicalunitbracket{adatnigǫha:ˀ} \trs{be wary, cautious}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

\cayuga{wadatnigǫ́ha:ˀ} \trs{it is wary, cautious}

\lexicalunitbracket{adęgǫnyǫhsd} \trs{be loyal, respectful}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hadęgǫnyǫ́hstaˀ} \trs{he is loyal} (to the cause), \trs{he is respectful}

\lexicalunitbracket{adeksaˀdǫni} \trs{be childish}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{ǫdeksaˀdǫ́:nih} \trs{she is childish}

\lexicalunitbracket{adih} \trs{go in a direction}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

\cayuga{tgáęgwadih} \trs{they are going in a direction}

\lexicalunitbracket{adǫh} \trs{say}

\cayuga{ǫ́:dǫh} \trs{she says} (also see the full paradigm on page \pageref{figtab:1:say})


\lexicalunitbracket{adǫwihsriyaˀgs} \trs{be out of breath, dying}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hadǫwi̱hsri:yaˀs} \trs{he is out of breath}, \trs{he is dying}

\lexicalunitbracket{adǫwihsroˀkd} \trs{be out of breath}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hadǫwi̱hsróˀktaˀ} \trs{he is out of breath}

\lexicalunitbracket{adwęnadeni, adwęnadeny} \trs{be near puberty}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{dehadwęnádęnyǫhs} \trs{he is reaching puberty}, (literally, \trs{his voice is changing})

\lexicalunitbracket{atgwadǫ} \trs{weave, zig-zag about}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hatgwá:dǫh} \trs{he is zig-zagging}

\lexicalunitbracket{atwajiyǫnih} \trs{barren}, with \stem{{\negative}}

\cayuga{tęˀ deyǫtwaji:yǫ́:nih} \trs{she is barren}

\lexicalunitbracket{atwęnaga:dad} \trs{interpreter}

\cayuga{hadęwęnagá:da:s} \trs{he is an interpreter}

\lexicalunitbracket{e:hah} \trs{proud}

\cayuga{igé:hah} \trs{I am gloating, boastful}

\lexicalunitbracket{ę:hęh} \trs{speak carelessly}, with \stem{{\translocative},{\repetitive}}

\cayuga{hehshawęhę́h gwáˀe:ˀ} \trs{he is speaking without thinking again as usual} \stem{gwáˀ-e:ˀ} \trs{really-again}

\lexicalunitbracket{haˀdatęhs} \trs{be thirsty}

\cayuga{shaˀdá:tęhs} \trs{you are thirsty}

\lexicalunitbracket{hyadǫhsraędiˀ} \trs{be smart, educated} (book-educated)

\cayuga{syadǫ̱hsráędiˀ} \trs{you are smart} (book-educated)

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫwęhdraˀ} \trs{be cantankerous}

\cayuga{enǫ́wę̱hdraˀ} \trs{she is cantankerous}

\end{multicols}


\subsection{Verbs taking \textsc{p}-series personal prefixes, stative aspect only}
\begin{multicols}{2}



\lexicalunitbracket{adagaideˀ} \trs{well, healthy, fine}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{agadagáideˀ} \trs{I am well, fine, healthy}

\lexicalunitbracket{adagaideˀ} \trs{feel sick}, with \stem{{\negative},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{tęˀ desadagáideˀ} \trs{you feel sick}

\lexicalunitbracket{adehsˀǫh} \trs{ready}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{sadéhsˀǫh?} \trs{Are you ready?} (this might be an Onondaga word)

\lexicalunitbracket{adehsrǫnihsˀǫh} \trs{ready}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{agade̱hsrǫ́ni̱hsˀǫh} \trs{I am ready}

\lexicalunitbracket{adeˀka:ˀ} \trs{hen-pecked}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hodéˀka:ˀ} \trs{he is hen-pecked}

\lexicalunitbracket{adenǫhahe:ˀ} \trs{happy}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hodonǫ̱háhe:ˀ} \trs{he is happy}

\lexicalunitbracket{adetsę:} \trs{glutton}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hodé:tsę:} \trs{he is a glutton}



\lexicalunitbracket{adiˀgrǫˀ} \trs{shy}

\cayuga{godíˀgrǫˀ} \trs{she is shy}


\lexicalunitbracket{adǫnhi:ˀ} \trs{enjoy life}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{agádǫnhi:} \trs{I am alive}, \trs{I am born}, \trs{I am full of life}

\lexicalunitbracket{adǫnhoˀg} \trs{premature, mentally challenged}, with \stem{{\cislocative},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{todǫ́:nhoˀk} \trs{he is mentally challenged}, \trs{he was born premature}

\lexicalunitbracket{adǫtgadeˀ} \trs{happy}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{odǫ́tgadeˀ} \trs{it is fun, a good feeling}

\lexicalunitbracket{adǫtgadeˀ} \trs{unhappy}, with \stem{{\negative},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{de̱ˀagadǫ́tgadeˀ, dewagadǫ́tgadǫˀ} \trs{I am not happy}


\lexicalunitbracket{adrihodahǫh} \trs{confused}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{dewagadrihodáhǫh} \trs{I am confused or mixed up}, \trs{something is blocking my thinking}

\lexicalunitbracket{adrihodahse:ˀ} \trs{confused}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{dewagadrihodáhse:ˀ} \trs{I am confused}, \trs{I cannot make up my mind}

\lexicalunitbracket{adrihowi:} \trs{slow, slow-moving, clumsy}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hodrihó:wi:} \trs{he is clumsy}

\lexicalunitbracket{adrihwagwaihshǫ} \trs{believable, credible, righteous, fair, honest, noble}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{godrihwagwáihshǫh} \trs{she is fair, righteous}

\lexicalunitbracket{agyaˀdadaihę:} \trs{be hot} (person)

\cayuga{agyaˀdadáihę:} \trs{I am hot}

\lexicalunitbracket{agyaˀdanegaǫ, agyaˀdanega:} \trs{hernia}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{dewagagyaˀdanégaǫ} \trs{I have a hernia}

\lexicalunitbracket{agyanaˀǫh} \trs{possessed, addicted}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hogyána̱ˀǫh} \trs{he is possessed, addicted} (with gambling, women, etc.)

\lexicalunitbracket{agyaod} \trs{have a tent up}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hogyáot} \trs{he has put up a tent}


\lexicalunitbracket{agyę} \trs{quiet}, with \stem{{\contrastive},{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{taˀdésagyę:} \trs{you are quiet}

\lexicalunitbracket{agyesaˀgeh} \trs{generous}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{gogyésa̱ˀgeh} \trs{she is generous, generous to a fault}

\lexicalunitbracket{agyesahsdǫ:} \trs{extravagant, wasteful}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{gogyéhsa̱hsdǫ:} \trs{she is extravagant, wasteful}

\lexicalunitbracket{ahgahę:} \trs{jealous}

\cayuga{go̱hgáhę:} \trs{she is jealous}

\lexicalunitbracket{ahsdęhyai} \trs{be an older woman}

\cayuga{gohsdę́hyai} \trs{she is an older woman}

\lexicalunitbracket{ahsę:} \trs{fat}

\cayuga{agáhsę:} \trs{I am fat}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ogǫ́hsa̱hsę:} \trs{it has a fat face}

\lexicalunitbracket{ahshę:} \trs{slow-moving}

\cayuga{agáhshę:} \trs{I am slow to act}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ohnyáhshę:} \trs{slow beat}

\lexicalunitbracket{aknigǫhnyaˀgǫh} \trs{grieve, be broken-hearted}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{dewaknigǫ́hnya̱ˀgǫh} \trs{I am broken-hearted, grieving}

\lexicalunitbracket{anhęhod} \trs{pee all the time}

\cayuga{gonhę́ho:t} \trs{she pees all the time}

\lexicalunitbracket{asdę:ˀęh} \trs{be old} (living thing)

\cayuga{hohsdę́:ˀęh} \trs{he is old}, \trs{he is an old man}

\lexicalunitbracket{atetgędǫni:} \trs{moody, be in a bad mood}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{hotehtgędǫ́:ni:} \trs{he is in a funny or odd mood}, \trs{he is moody}

\lexicalunitbracket{atgehd} \trs{have something around one’s neck}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{satgéhdǫh} \trs{you have it around your neck}

\lexicalunitbracket{atgeˀi:ˀ} \trs{have tangled hair}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{dewagatgéˀi:ˀ} \trs{my hair is tangled}

\lexicalunitbracket{atgeˀogw} \trs{have messy hair}, \trs{scattered clothes, rags}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{desatgeˀó:gwęh} \trs{you have rumpled hair, ruffled hair}

\lexicalunitbracket{atgǫˀ} \trs{have evil or dangerous power, have bad medicine, be a witch, warlock, be sacred}

\cayuga{gotgǫˀ} \trs{she is a witch}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{odrę́natgǫˀ} \trs{sacred songs}

\lexicalunitbracket{atnegad} \trs{crooked, not level, tipsy}, with \stem{{\negative},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{disa:tné:ga:t} \trs{you are not level, you are tipsy}

\lexicalunitbracket{atnigǫhadogę:} \trs{undecided, indecisive}, with \stem{{\negative}}

\cayuga{desaˀnigǫhadó:gę:} \trs{you cannot decide which way to go, you are flighty}

\lexicalunitbracket{atnigǫhadogę:} \trs{immature}, with \stem{{\negative},{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{desatnigǫhadó:gęh} \trs{you are immature in mind}

\lexicalunitbracket{atnǫhahe:ˀ} \trs{wearing a wig}

\cayuga{gonǫ́hahe:ˀ} \trs{she has a wig on}

\lexicalunitbracket{atowinyǫˀse:} \trs{have a cold}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{gotowinyǫ́ˀse:} \trs{she has a cold}

\lexicalunitbracket{atsahnihd} \trs{industrious, tireless, active, ambitious, diligent, zealous}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{gotsáhniht} \trs{she is a good worker, tireless, active, industrious,etc.}

\lexicalunitbracket{awęh} \trs{have, own}

\cayuga{agá:węh} \trs{it is mine}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀdai:ˀ} \trs{dirty}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{de̱hóˀdaiˀ} \trs{he got dirty} (covered with manure)

\lexicalunitbracket{ędagę:} \trs{be cowardly, timid, weak, wimpy}

\cayuga{gowę́dagę:, agawędá:gę:} \trs{she is a wimp, timid}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęhsoweksǫ} \trs{be shod, have shoes on}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{de̱honę̱hsóweksǫˀ} \trs{they have their shoes on}

\lexicalunitbracket{e:ˀǫ:} \trs{will, decide}

\cayuga{hawé:ˀǫ:} \trs{he has willed}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnowę:} \trs{be a liar}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\cayuga{sęnó:wę:} \trs{you are a liar}

\lexicalunitbracket{ę:sǫ} \trs{be shod, have shoes on}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{de̱ho:wę́:sǫ:} \trs{he has the shoes on}


\lexicalunitbracket{gahagwaǫd} \trs{have a sty}

\subsection{Verbs taking \textsc{a}-series neuter prefixes, stative aspect only}

\lexicalunitbracket{aˀse:ˀ} \trs{doubled up}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\lexicalunitbracket{wihjih} \trs{overcooked}

\cayuga{owíhjih} \trs{it is overcooked}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdǫh} \trs{direction}

\cayuga{(tsęh) niyóya̱ˀdǫh} \trs{a direction}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdowehde:ˀ} \trs{contemplation}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\cayuga{deyoya̱ˀdówe̱hde:ˀ} \trs{to weigh the consequences}, \trs{it is brain-wracking}

\lexicalunitbracket{+yanoweˀ} \trs{fast}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ga̱ˀdrehdaya:nó:weˀ} \trs{train}, \trs{fast car}


\lexicalunitbracket{yanreˀ} \trs{good, nice, beautiful}

\cayuga{oyá:nreˀ} \trs{it is nice, good, beautiful}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaǫˀdatgę:} \trs{decomposed corpse}

\cayuga{oyaǫˀdá:tgę:} \trs{a state of decomposition}

\lexicalunitbracket{yędehd} \trs{recognizable, plain to be seen, conspicuous}

\cayuga{oyę́:deht} \trs{it is recognizable or plain to be seen, conspicuous}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫgyaˀd} \trs{laugh}, \trs{amusing, laughable}

\cayuga{oyǫ́:gyaˀt} \trs{it is amusing, laughable}


\end{multicols}

\subsection{Verbs taking \textsc{p}-series neuter prefixes, habitual aspect only}
\begin{multicols}{2}

\cayuga{deyóhyojihs} \trs{it is bitter, salty, sour}

\end{multicols}

\subsection{Conjugation of the irregular verb \stem{+e:s}, \stem{+i:s}, \stem{ǫ:s} \trs{long}}

\cayuga{The verb meaning} \trs{to be long} has several forms: it is \stem{ǫ:s} when it has no incorporated noun \xref{ex:longex1}. It most often takes the form of \stem{+e:s} when it has an incorporated noun \xref{ex:longex2}. However, with some incorporated nouns, the form is \stem{+i:s} instead of \stem{+e:s} \xref{ex:longex3}.

\ea\label{ex:longex1} \stem{ǫ:s} ‛long'
\ea í:yǫ:s \\
\gll í:-y-ǫ:s\\
\textsc{{\prothetic}-3s.a}-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛it is long'
\newpage
\ex tęˀ de̱ˀyǫ:s\\
\gll tęˀ de̱ˀ-y-ǫ:s\\ 
not \textsc{{\negative}-3s.a}-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛it is not long'
\ex niyǫ́:sˀah\\
\gll ni-y-ǫ́:s-ˀah\\
\textsc{{\partitive}-3s.a}-long.{\stative}-{\diminutive}\\
\glt ‛just a little bit long'
\ex ǫ́:sǫˀs\\
\gll ǫ́:s-ǫˀs\\
{\noprefix}-long.{\stative}-{\plural}\\
\glt ‛lengthy objects'
\z
\z

\ea\label{ex:longex2} \stem{+e:s} ‛long'
\ea onóˀje:s\\
\gll o-nóˀj-e:s\\
\textsc{3s.p}-tooth-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛fang'
\ex ganǫ́hse:s\\
\gll ga-nǫ́hs-e:s\\
\textsc{3s.a}-house-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛longhouse'

\ex ganǫhsé:sǫˀs\\
\gll ga-nǫhs-é:s-ǫˀs\\
\textsc{3s.a}-house-long.{\stative}-{\plural}\\
\glt ‛longhouses'

\ex hogéˀe:s\\
\gll ho-géˀ-e:s\\
\textsc{3s.m.p}-hair-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛he has long hair'

\z
\z

\ea\label{ex:longex3} \stem{+i:s} ‛long'
\ea gáęni:s\\
\gll gá-ęn-i:s \\
\textsc{3s.a}-song-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛long song' 

\newpage
\ex ohsdi:s\\
\gll o-hsd-is\\
\textsc{3s.p}-tool-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛trade cloth'

\ex oshái:s\\
\gll o-sh-á-i:s \\
\textsc{3s.p}-string-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛long string, rope'

\ex oháhi:s\\
\gll o-háh-i:s\\
\textsc{3s.p}-road-long.{\stative}\\
\glt ‛long row, road'

\z
\z




\subsection{Conjugation of \stem{+od} \trs{stand}, \stem{ǫd} \trs{attached, put in}}

The verbs \stem{+od} \trs{stand} and \stem{ǫd} \trs{attached, put in} are often part of fixed \textsc{nv} expressions (\sectref{Fixed and transparent expressions}). The following examples illustrate how these verbs are conjugated, using fixed \textsc{nv} expressions as examples.

\ea\label{ex:od.stand} \stem{+od} \trs{stand}
\ea \textsc{habitual} \stem{+ot-haˀ} stand-{\habitual}\\
\glll wadrę́notaˀ\\
wa-d-ręn-ot-haˀ\\
\textsc{3s.a}-{\semireflexive}-song-stand-{\habitual}\\
\glt \trs{stereo, radio}
\ex \textsc{habitual past} \stem{+ot-ha-hk} stand.{\habitual}-{\former}\\
\glll hadręnotahk \\
ha-d-ręn-ot-ha-hk\\
\textsc{3s.m.a}-{\semireflexive}-song-stand-{\habitual}-{\former}\\
\glt \trs{he used to be a singer, used to sing} 
\ex \textsc{indefinite habitual} \stem{a:-…ot-ha-hk} {\indefinite}-…stand.{\habitual}-{\former}\\
\glll a:gadręnota:k \\
a:-g-ad-ręn-ot-ha-:k \\
\textsc{{\indefinite}-1s.a}-{\semireflexive}-sont-stand-{\habitual}-{\modalizer}\\
\glt \trs{I would be a singer} 
\newpage
\ex \textsc{punctual} \stem{+od-ęˀ} stand-{\punctual}\\
\glll a:sejáodęˀ\\
a:-s-e-ja-od-ęˀ\\
\textsc{{\indefinite}-2s.a}-{\joinerE}-smoke-stand-{\punctual}\\
\glt \trs{you would smoke} 

\ex \textsc{stative} \stem{o:t} stand.{\stative}\\
\glll gona:drę́:no:t\\
gon-a:d-rę́:n-o:t\\
\textsc{3ns.fi.p}-{\semireflexive}-song-stand.{\stative}\\
\glt \trs{they are singing}
\ex \textsc{stative past} \stem{+od-a-ˀk} stand-\textsc{{\joinerA}-{\former}}\\
\glll gonadręnó:daˀk \\
gon-ad-ręn-ó:d-a-ˀk\\
\textsc{3ns.fi.p}-{\semireflexive}-song-stand.\textsc{stative-joinerA-former}\\
\glt \trs{they did sing} 
\ex \textsc{stative progressive} \stem{+od-a-gy-e-ˀ} stand-\textsc{joinerA-{\progressive}}-go-{\stative}\\ 
\glll honadręnódagyeˀ \\
hon-ad-ręn-ód-a-gy-e-ˀ\\
\textsc{3ns.m.p}-{\semireflexive}-song-stand-\textsc{joinerA-{\progressive}}-go-{\stative}\\
\glt \trs{they are singing a song as they travel} 
\z
\z

\ea\label{ex:od.attached} \stem{ǫd} \trs{attached, put in}
\ea \textsc{habitual} \stem{ǫt-haˀ}  attached-{\habitual}\\
\glll Hahsdawędrǫ:taˀ \\
ha-hsdawędr-ǫt-haˀ \\
\textsc{3s.m.a}-rattle-attach-{\habitual}\\
\glt \trs{Attaching Rattles} (Mohawk Chief Title)
\ex \textsc{punctual} \stem{ǫd-ęˀ} attached-{\punctual}\\
\glll ęhsade̱ˀsgǫ́:dęˀ\\
ę-hs-ad-e̱-ˀsg-ǫ́:d-ęˀ\\
\textsc{future-2s.a-{\semireflexive}}-{\joinerE}-roast-put.in-{\punctual}\\
\glt \trs{you will roast} 
\ex \textsc{}stative \stem{ǫ:t} attached.{\stative}\\
\glll wadéˀsgǫ:t \\
wa-d-é-ˀsg-ǫ:t\\
\textsc{3s.a-{\semireflexive}}-{\joinerE}-roast-attached.{\stative}\\
\glt \trs{it is roasting, frying}
\ex \textsc{stative past} \stem{ǫd-a-ˀk} attached-\textsc{{\joinerA}-{\former}}\\
\glll gotnaˀdáǫdaˀk\\
go-t-naˀdá-ǫd-a-ˀk\\
\textsc{3s.fi.p}-{\semireflexive}-bread-put.in-\textsc{{\joinerA}-{\former}}\\
\glt \trs{she made bread} 
\z
\z


\section{Three-aspect verbs} \label{three-aspect verbs}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{haˀwatnegátsˀaht} \trs{water is all gone}

\lexicalunitbracket{atsihsˀ} \trs{ripen}

{\habitual} \cayuga{watsíhsˀahs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awátsihsˀa:ˀ} \trs{it did mature} (as in plants), \trs{it completed its life-cycle}

{\stative} \cayuga{otsíhsˀǫh} \trs{it is done for the season}, \trs{it has gone full cycle}, \trs{it is mature}, \trs{they (plants) have finished out}

\lexicalunitbracket{atsihsę:} \trs{ripe}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awátsihsę:ˀ} \trs{it ripened for harvesting}

{\stative} \cayuga{otsíhshę:} \trs{it is at a mature state}

\lexicalunitbracket{atsotwahs} \trs{jump, hop}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{dewátsotwahs} \trs{fleas}, (literally, \trs{it jumps, hops})

\lexicalunitbracket{atwadased} \trs{encircle something (the calendar year)}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęwatwada:sé:dahk} \trs{it will encircle it} (speaking of the calendar year)

\lexicalunitbracket{+dase} \trs{whirl, swirl around} (fluid, air), with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degawá:dasehs} \trs{tornado}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atgahnegádase:ˀ} \trs{hydrologic cycle, water cycle}

{\stative} \cayuga{ohnawadá:se:} \trs{whirlpool}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀdrehdahetgęˀ} \trs{break down} (said of vehicles)

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgeˀdre̱hdáhetgęˀ} \trs{my car broke down}

{\stative} \cayuga{odrehda̱hétgę̱ˀǫh} \trs{a car is broken down}

\lexicalunitbracket{ędajihs} \trs{twilight}

{\habitual} \cayuga{wędá:jihs} \trs{dusk, twilight}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnihoˀg} \trs{lightning}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{dewę́ni̱hoks, dewę́ni̱hoˀs} \trs{it is lightning}

{\punctual} \cayuga{adwę́ni̱hoˀk} \trs{lightning struck}


\lexicalunitbracket{ęhnihsriyohs} \trs{improve, get nice} (weather)

{\punctual} \cayuga{sawęhni̱hsrí:yohs} \trs{it became a nice day again}


\lexicalunitbracket{ęnǫwaę} \trs{sink}

{\habitual} \cayuga{węnǫwáęhęˀ} \trs{it sinks} (all the time)

{\punctual} \cayuga{awęnowáęˀ} \trs{it sank}

{\stative} \cayuga{onáwaęˀ} \trs{it has sunk in liquid}

\lexicalunitbracket{ga:hgwę} \trs{sunset}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hegáhgwęˀs} \trs{to the setting sun, the direction of the sunset, west}

{\punctual} \cayuga{haˀgáhgwęˀ} \trs{sunset}, \trs{the sun went down}

\lexicalunitbracket{gęnhǫdi, gęnhǫgy} \trs{summer}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęyogęnhǫ́:diˀ} \trs{it will be summer}

\lexicalunitbracket{gowanheˀ} \trs{become big}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agagowá:nheˀ} \trs{it became big}

\lexicalunitbracket{hehdagahatw} \trs{plough}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ga̱hehdagáhatwahs} \trs{plow}

{\stative} \cayuga{ga̱hehdagáhatwęh} \trs{ploughed field}

\lexicalunitbracket{hnegagyęhętw} \trs{low tide}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\cislocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dętgahnegagyę̱hę:toˀ} \trs{it will be low tide}

\lexicalunitbracket{hnegahe:ˀ} \trs{high tide}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ętgahnegáhe:k} \trs{it will be high tide}

\lexicalunitbracket{hretgęˀ} \trs{go bad, spoil} (said of ideas)

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwáhetgęˀ} \trs{it (an idea) will spoil, go bad}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsdaędaˀ} \trs{stop raining}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agahsdáędaˀ} \trs{it stopped raining}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsdaowanahd} \trs{rain hard}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agasdáowanaht} \trs{it rained hard}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsdaowanęh} \trs{rain hard}

{\stative} \cayuga{gahsdaowá:nęh} \trs{it is raining hard}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsgęˀdrǫd} \trs{rusting, mouldy}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awahsgę̱ˀdrǫ́:dę:ˀ} \trs{it got mouldy}, \trs{it got rusty}

\lexicalunitbracket{+ihęh} \trs{shake}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} {\punctual} \cayuga{agyǫhwęjáihęh} \trs{earthquake}, (literally, \trs{the land shook})

\lexicalunitbracket{ihnodǫ} \trs{flood}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awęhnó:dǫ:ˀ} \trs{flood}, \trs{it flooded}

{\stative} \cayuga{ohnó:dǫˀ} \trs{it is flooded}

\lexicalunitbracket{jiˀdaga:, jiˀdagai} \trs{whining, crying sound}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degajiˀdá:ga:} \trs{a whiner, cryer}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atgajiˀdágai} \trs{(there was) whining, crying, repetitive complaining}

\lexicalunitbracket{jihsdaˀdr} \trs{go with the fire}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęseji̱hsdáˀdraˀ} \trs{you will go with the fire} (refers to the Gaihwi:yo: convention)

{\stative} \cayuga{hodiji̱hsdáˀdrǫ:} \trs{they have gone to the fire} (refers to the Gaihwi:yo: convention)


\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnhęhtsędǫh} \trs{wag one’s tail}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\stative} \cayuga{deyoˀnhęhtsę́dǫ̱hǫh} \trs{it is wagging its tail}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnǫ:} \trs{removed}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

{\stative} \cayuga{gyonǫ:} \trs{it has been removed}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫˀa:ga:, nǫˀa:gai} \trs{noise made by banging head}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\repetitive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsganǫˀa:gái} \trs{there will be heads banging}

{\stative} \cayuga{desganǫˀá:ga:} \trs{a head banging}


\lexicalunitbracket{nǫnhe} \trs{fill up}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ganǫ́:nheˀs} \trs{it fills up all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agánǫnheˀ} \trs{it filled up}


\lexicalunitbracket{ǫhwęjaihęh} \trs{earthquake}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agyǫhwęjáihęh} \trs{earthquake}, (literally, \trs{the land shook})

\lexicalunitbracket{rihsdiˀdr} \trs{survey}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hadíhsdi̱ˀdrehs} \trs{they are surveying the land}, \trs{surveyors}

{\stative} \cayuga{gaíhsdi̱ˀdrǫ:} \trs{it has been surveyed}

\lexicalunitbracket{rihwahdǫˀ} \trs{die out, become extinct}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agaihwáhdǫˀ} \trs{it became extinct, died out} (old word, said of ideas)

{\stative} \cayuga{oíhwahdǫˀǫh} \trs{it is extinct}

\lexicalunitbracket{rihwędaˀ} \trs{wear out}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agaihwę́:daˀ} \trs{it wore out} (i.e. clothing)

\lexicalunitbracket{+tęhsd} \trs{dry up, evaporate}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{sagaga̱hóˀjatęhs} \trs{the grass dried up}

\lexicalunitbracket{waęhęwiˀ} \trs{hurricane}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gawaęhę́:wiˀ} \trs{hurricane}

\lexicalunitbracket{waˀnęda:ˀg} \trs{stick to, cling to}

{\habitual} \cayuga{owaˀnę́:da:s} \trs{it sticks to it}, \trs{it adheres to it}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀowa̱ˀnę́:da:ˀk, aˀowaˀnę:da:ˀ} \trs{it is stuck}

{\stative} \cayuga{owaˀnędá:gǫh} \trs{it is stuck on something}

\lexicalunitbracket{wa:nohsd} \trs{become cold, cool} (weather)

{\punctual} \cayuga{sagawá:nohs} \trs{it became cooler}

{\stative} \cayuga{owa:nóhsdǫh} \trs{it got cold (weather)}

\lexicalunitbracket{wędęnawę:} \trs{become a wet day}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awędęnáwę:} \trs{it got wet}, \trs{the day got wet}

\lexicalunitbracket{yagęhdahgw} \trs{come out suddenly}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dagayagę́hdahk} \trs{it came out} (suddenly)

\lexicalunitbracket{yędaˀ} \trs{settle}, with \stem{{\translocative},{\cislocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hatgayę́:daˀ} \trs{it is settled}

\lexicalunitbracket{yędehte} \trs{emerge unintentionally}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀǫyędéhteˀ} \trs{it emerged unintentionally}

\lexicalunitbracket{yesh} \trs{be too bad}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agayeshaˀ} \trs{it is too bad}


\lexicalunitbracket{weodę} \trs{become mouldy}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agawéodęˀ} \trs{it got mouldy}

\end{multicols}

\subsubsection*{List of three-aspect weather verbs}

The thematic category of weather verbs is listed in this section for convenience. They are three-aspect verbs taking neuter prefixes.

\begin{multicols}{2}

\lexicalunitnobracket{agahsdáędaˀ} \trs{it stopped raining}
\lexicalunitnobracket{agasdaowá:naht} \trs{it rained hard}
\lexicalunitnobracket{awáyǫgyǫ:} \trs{it is drizzling}, \trs{misty rain}, \trs{fine rain}
\lexicalunitnobracket{awędęnáwę:} \trs{it got wet}, \trs{the day got wet}
\lexicalunitnobracket{degawá:dasehs} \trs{tornado}
\lexicalunitnobracket{dewadewayędáǫhaˀ} \trs{it is thundering}
\lexicalunitnobracket{dewęni̱hóˀksǫh} \trs{lightening}
\lexicalunitnobracket{deyotgręgrę́hdǫh} \trs{the sky is dreary, grey}
\lexicalunitnobracket{deyotsadáęˀ} \trs{it is foggy}
\lexicalunitnobracket{deyoyęgwáę:ˀ} \trs{it is a smoky or hazy day}
\lexicalunitnobracket{ęyohsdáǫdiˀ} \trs{it is going to rain}
\lexicalunitnobracket{ęyoˀgrǫ́:diˀ} \trs{it will snow}
\lexicalunitnobracket{gahsdaowá:nęh} \trs{it is raining hard}
\lexicalunitnobracket{gawa:shá:sdeˀ} \trs{strong winds}
\lexicalunitnobracket{gawaęhę́:wiˀ} \trs{hurricane}
\lexicalunitnobracket{gawaowá:nęh} \trs{big wind}
\lexicalunitnobracket{odaˀgradé:nyǫ:} \trs{there are snow flurries}
\lexicalunitnobracket{odę́haǫt} \trs{sunshine}
\lexicalunitnobracket{odesdá:denyǫ:} \trs{it is sprinkling}
\lexicalunitnobracket{odrǫ́hyo:t} \trs{rainbow}
\lexicalunitnobracket{ogahgwędǫ́:gyǫ:} \trs{it is snowing snow pellets}
\lexicalunitnobracket{ohjíˀgreˀ} \trs{it is cloudy}
\lexicalunitnobracket{onaˀnawę́ˀǫh} \trs{it has thawed, melted}
\lexicalunitnobracket{onáˀno:ˀ} \trs{it is cold, cool}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oné:nǫˀ} \trs{it is mild, warm}, \trs{a warm or hot day}
\lexicalunitnobracket{aǫgo̱hdǫ́h oné:nǫˀ} \trs{it is exceptionally hot} (weather)
\lexicalunitnobracket{onǫnyáędagyeˀ sadaǫgyǫ:} \trs{freezing rain}
\lexicalunitnobracket{onǫ́nyaęˀ} \trs{it is frozen}
\lexicalunitnobracket{onyęˀgwadá:se:} \trs{drifting snow}
\lexicalunitnobracket{osdáǫ:} \trs{it looks like rain}
\lexicalunitnobracket{osdáǫgyǫ:} \trs{it is raining}
\lexicalunitnobracket{otó:weˀ} \trs{it is cold}
\lexicalunitnobracket{otsádę̱ˀǫh} \trs{it is damp}
\lexicalunitnobracket{owa:dáihę:} \trs{warm wind}
\lexicalunitnobracket{owá:deˀ} \trs{windy}, \trs{wind}, \trs{it is a breeze}
\lexicalunitnobracket{owá:nǫ:} \trs{cold wind}
\lexicalunitnobracket{owa:nóhsdǫh} \trs{it got cold} (weather)
\lexicalunitnobracket{owídrǫgyǫ:} \trs{it is hailing}, \trs{sleet}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀáwayeˀ} \trs{dew}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀawayǫ́:gyǫ:} \trs{it is drizzling}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀdáihę:} \trs{a hot day}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀgrǫ:} \trs{it looks like snow}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀgrǫ́:gyǫ:} \trs{it is snowing}
\lexicalunitnobracket{oˀgrowanáhdǫh} \trs{it is snowing hard}
\lexicalunitnobracket{wę̱hnihsrí:yo:} \trs{it is a nice day}
\end{multicols}

\subsection{Three-aspect verbs taking \textsc{p}-series neuter prefixes}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{adeg} \trs{burn up}

{\habitual} \cayuga{odé:kaˀ} \trs{fire}, \trs{it is burning}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyó:de:k} \trs{it will burn}

{\stative} \cayuga{odé:gęh} \trs{it is burnt}

\lexicalunitbracket{aˀgrǫdi, aˀgrǫgy} \trs{snow}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyoˀgrǫ́:diˀ} \trs{it will snow}

{\stative} \cayuga{oˀgrǫ́:gyǫ:} \trs{it is snowing}

\lexicalunitbracket{aˀgrowanahd} \trs{snow hard}

{\stative} \cayuga{oˀgrowanáhdǫh} \trs{it is snowing hard}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęh, ęˀ} \trs{happen}, with \stem{{\partitive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{niyá:węhs} \trs{how it happens}

{\punctual} \cayuga{nęyá:węh} \trs{it will happen}

{\stative} \cayuga{niyáwę̱ˀǫh} \trs{how it did happen}

\lexicalunitbracket{hę} \trs{be day}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyó:hęˀ} \trs{it will be tomorrow}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsdagwaę} \trs{dirty, soiled}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀohsdagwáę:} \trs{it got dirty or soiled}

{\stative} \cayuga{ohsdágwaę:} \trs{it is soiled, dirty, stained}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsdaǫdi, hsdaǫgy} \trs{rain}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyohsdáǫdiˀ} \trs{it is going to rain}

{\stative} \cayuga{osdáǫgyǫ:} \trs{it is raining}

\lexicalunitbracket{hsgęˀdraę} \trs{get rusty}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ohsgę́ˀdraę:s} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyohsgęˀdráę:} \trs{it will get rusty}

{\stative} \cayuga{ohsgę́ˀdraeˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ka} \trs{leak}

{\habitual} \cayuga{okahs} \trs{it leaks}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyó:kaˀ} \trs{it will leak}

\lexicalunitbracket{nihsheˀ} \trs{a length of time, duration}

{\punctual} \cayuga{tsaˀóni̱hsheˀ} \trs{a long time, for that length of time, while, during the time that}

\lexicalunitbracket{nyahęh, nyahęˀ} \trs{boil}

{\habitual} \cayuga{onyáhęhs} \trs{it is boiling}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgyǫ́nya̱hęh} \trs{it will boil}

{\stative} \cayuga{onyáhę̱ˀǫh} \trs{it has boiled}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫhwęhsdaga:} \trs{make a wheezing noise}

{\stative} \cayuga{ohwę́hsdaga:} \trs{it is wheezing}

\lexicalunitbracket{tgęh, tgęˀ} \trs{become rotten}

{\habitual} \cayuga{otgę́hs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀó:tgęh} \trs{it became spoiled, rotten}

{\stative} {otgę́ˀǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{tsihsdęh, tsihsdęˀ} \trs{get numb}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀótsihsdęh} \trs{it got numb}

{\stative} \cayuga{otsíhsdę̱ˀǫh} \trs{it is numb}

\end{multicols}

\subsection{Three-aspect verbs taking personal prefixes, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}

\subsubsection*{A-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{adadahsha:gwę, adadahsha:gwani} \trs{make oneself remember , remind onself}, with \stem{{\cislocative},{\reflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ętsadadahshá:gwęˀ} \trs{you will remind yourself, make yourself remember}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadehsnye} \trs{groom oneself, prepare oneself mentally, look after oneself, tidy oneself up}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\reflexive}}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desadadéhsnyeh} \trs{tidy up!} \trs{groom yourself!}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadrihǫnyanih, adadrihǫnyę} \trs{read}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ǫdadri̱hǫ́nyanih} \trs{she is reading}

{\stative} \cayuga{wadadri̱hǫ́nyani:} \trs{reading material}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sadadri̱hó:nyęh} \trs{read!}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadrihwagwenyaˀs} \trs{be a success}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahsadadrihwagwé:nyaˀs} \trs{you are a success}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadrihwagwenyęˀs} \trs{achieve something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsadadrihwagwé:nyęˀs} \trs{you will achieve}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadrihwahdǫˀd} \trs{commit suidice}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awadadríhwa̱hdǫˀt} \trs{suicide}, (literally, \trs{someone did away with themselves})

\lexicalunitbracket{adadriyo} \trs{kill oneself, commit suicide}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awadadrí:yoˀ} \trs{it killed itself}, \trs{suicide}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadrohegę} \trs{accumulate for oneself}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsadadrohé:gęˀ} \trs{you will accumulate (things, ideas, etc.) for yourself}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadwędehd, adadwędehd} \trs{forfeit one’s life, give up one’s life}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}/\stem{{\reflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sadwę́dehtaˀ} \trs{you forfeit things all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{asa:dwę́:deht} \trs{you forfeited}

{\punctual} \cayuga{awadadwę́:deht} \trs{it (a pet) forfeited its life}

\lexicalunitbracket{adadwiyahdǫˀd} \trs{have an abortion}, with \stem{{\reflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ǫdadwiyáhdǫtaˀ} \trs{abortion}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agadadwíya̱hdǫˀt} \trs{I had an abortion}

{\stative} \cayuga{agadadwiya̱hdǫ́ˀdǫh} \trs{I did have an abortion}

\lexicalunitbracket{adaˀgehod} \trs{have, get an erection}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhadage̱hó:dęˀ} \trs{he will get an erection}

{\stative} \cayuga{sadáˀge̱ho:t} \trs{you have an erection}

\lexicalunitbracket{adagyaˀdahgwaˀd} \trs{do push ups}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\reflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degaǫdagya̱ˀdáhgwa̱ˀtaˀ} \trs{they are doing push ups}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgaǫdagya̱ˀdáhgwaˀt} \trs{they will do push ups}

\lexicalunitbracket{adagyenaw, adagyenaǫ, adagyena:} \trs{wrestle}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\reflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{de̱hęnada:gyé:nahs} \trs{wrestlers}, \trs{they are wrestling}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsadagyé:na:ˀ} \trs{you will wrestle}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desadagyé:na:} \trs{you wrestle!}

\lexicalunitbracket{adahgahsdǫ, adahgahsd} \trs{endure}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sadáhgahstaˀ} \trs{you do endure}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsada̱hgáhsdǫˀ} \trs{you will tough it out, endure}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sadáhga̱hsdǫ:} \trs{you endure!}, \trs{go and cook in the cookhouse!}

\lexicalunitbracket{adahgwaę} \trs{store something}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sadahgwáęhęˀ} \trs{you store things all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{asada̱hgwáęˀ} \trs{you did store it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sadáhgwaęˀ} \trs{store it, hold on to it temporarily!}

\lexicalunitbracket{adahihsd} \trs{prevent}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gadáhihstaˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgadahíhsdę} \trs{I will prevent}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desadodáisiˀ} \trs{you comb your hair}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewagęniya̱ˀgyáˀgǫh} \trs{I am burping, belching}


\lexicalunitbracket{enǫ} \trs{originate from someplace, come from someplace}, with \stem{{\partitive},{\cislocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{nita:wé:nǫh} \trs{a male stranger}, \trs{he is that age} (literally, \trs{where he comes from})

{\stative} \cayuga{nigya:wé:nǫ:} \trs{where it came from}

\lexicalunitbracket{enǫ} \trs{go to some unspecified place}, with \stem{{\contrastive}}

{\stative} \cayuga{tiyo:né:nǫ:} \trs{where they have gone}

\lexicalunitbracket{enǫ-gy-e} \trs{move forward}, with \cayuga{ohę́:dǫ:} \trs{ahead} \stem{{\translocative}}

{\stative}-{\progressive} \cayuga{ohę:dǫ́: heˀsénǫgyeˀ} \trs{you are moving forward}

\lexicalunitbracket{enǫ-gy-e} \trs{roam about randomly}, with \stem{{\contrastive}}

{\habitual}-{\progressive} \cayuga{tigęnenǫ́:gyeˀs} \trs{they are roaming about}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnohgra:ˀ} \trs{cause an allergic reaction, give someone a rash}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gowę́no̱hgra:ˀs} \trs{poison ivy}, \trs{any plant that causes a skin infection}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsawęnóhgra:ˀ} \trs{it will give you an allergic reaction}

{\stative} \cayuga{agęno̱hgrá:ˀǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnǫhwed, anǫhwed} \trs{stay overnight}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gęnǫ́weta}ˀ, \cayuga{ganǫ́wetaˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgę́nǫ̱hwe:t ęgánǫ̱hwe:t} \trs{I will stay overnight}

{\stative} \cayuga{agęnǫhwé:dǫh}, \cayuga{aganǫhwé:dǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnǫhwehstaˀ} \trs{bedroom} (literally, \trs{place to stay overnight}), with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{onǫ́hwehstaˀ} \trs{bedroom}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnoˀsgwi, onoˀsgwi} \trs{sweep}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degóno̱ˀsgwihs} \trs{I am sweeping}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgę́no̱ˀsgwiˀ} \trs{I will sweep}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewagęnóˀsgwi:} \trs{I have swept}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desę́no̱ˀsgwih} \trs{sweep!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęˀnowaę} \trs{squat}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsęˀnǫwáęˀ} \trs{you will squat, hunch down} (as for Gayędowa:nęh Peach Pit Game)

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnǫwaęd} \trs{sink something}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agęnǫwáędahk} \trs{I made it sink}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęnowęhd} \trs{tell a lie}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agę:nó:węht} \trs{I lied}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęˀnya:} \trs{govern, watch, look after}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{dehsę́ˀnya:ˀ} \trs{you are looking after it right now}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atsę́ˀnya:ˀ} \trs{you looked after it}


\lexicalunitbracket{ęnyahaˀd} \trs{boil something}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sęnyáhaˀt} \trs{boil it!}


\lexicalunitbracket{ęˀnyaˀwe, ęˀnyaˀo} \trs{clap}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desę́ˀnya̱ˀwe:k, desę́ˀnya̱ˀo:k} \trs{you clap!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ę:sętw} \trs{kick something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gę́:sętwahs} \trs{I am kicking}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgę:hsę́:toˀ} \trs{I will kick it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agę:sę́:twęh} \trs{I did kick it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sę:sę́:toh} \trs{kick it!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ęˀtsigahgyaˀg} \trs{cartwheel}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{desęˀtsihgáhgyaˀks} \trs{you do cartwheels}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęsęˀtsigáhgyaˀk} \trs{you will do a cartwheel}

\end{multicols}

\subsubsection*{G-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{g} \trs{eat}

{\habitual} \cayuga{í:ge:s} \trs{I eat}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ę́:ge:k} \trs{I will eat}

{\stative}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{agáhyagǫh} \trs{I am eating fruit}

\lexicalunitbracket{+gadad} \trs{raise up something}

{\habitual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{wadahsgwagá:da:s} \trs{lift bridge}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ędwaęnágada:t} \trs{we all will raise the song}


\lexicalunitbracket{ga:dǫ} \trs{tell a story}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęge:gá:dǫ:ˀ} \trs{I will tell a story}

{\stative} \cayuga{age:gá:dǫˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{segá:dǫ:} \trs{tell a story!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ga:gwahd} \trs{collect money}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ega:gwáhtaˀ} \trs{(someone collects money)}

\lexicalunitbracket{ga:gweni, ga:gweny} \trs{afford}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgega:gwé:niˀ} \trs{I will afford it}




\lexicalunitbracket{gahadeni, gahadeny} \trs{turn something on}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desega̱ha:dé:nih} \trs{turn it on!} (involves movement)

\lexicalunitbracket{gahdrǫni} \trs{stare}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sagahdrǫ́:nihs} \trs{you are staring at it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sagahdrǫ́:ni:} \trs{you are nosy, always looking)}, \trs{gape}, \trs{stare!}

\lexicalunitbracket{gahęd} \trs{drill, hole}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahadigahę́:dęˀ} \trs{they made a hole}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{segahę́:dęˀ} \trs{drill!}

\lexicalunitbracket{gahędęhd} \trs{hull berries}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsega̱hę́:dęht} \trs{you will hull berries}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsega̱héhgyaˀk} \trs{you will hull berries}

\lexicalunitbracket{ganęd} \trs{lick}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhséganę:t} \trs{you will lick it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{segá:nę:t} \trs{you lick!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ganyaˀg} \trs{pay}

{\stative}-{\progressive} \cayuga{goganya̱ˀkdǫ́hǫgyeˀ} \trs{she is paying as the goes along}

\lexicalunitbracket{gaˀtsy} \trs{take off, remove}

\lexicalunitbracket{gę} \trs{look ahead, forsee}, with \cayuga{ohę:dǫh} \trs{ahead} and \stem{{\translocative}}

\lexicalunitbracket{ged} \trs{grate, scrape, file}

\lexicalunitbracket{gędr, gęse:} \trs{skim off, scrape off}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewagegę́:drǫ:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\habitual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}}  \cayuga{dewahahágędrǫhs} \trs{road scraper, grader}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{dęsewidrágędrǫ:ˀ} \trs{you will take the cream off, skim the milk}

\lexicalunitbracket{gęihsd} \trs{move, postpone}

{\habitual} \cayuga{segę́ihstaˀ} \trs{you postpone it all the time}, \trs{you move it all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ędwa:gę́is} \trs{we all will postpone}

{\stative} \cayuga{sagę́ihsdǫh} \trs{you have postponed it}

\lexicalunitbracket{getsgw} \trs{raise to a vertical position, give a party}

{\habitual} \cayuga{segé:tsgwahs} \trs{you are lifting it to a vertical position}, \trs{you give parties}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhségetsgoˀ} \trs{you will lift things to a vertical position}

{\stative} \cayuga{gyagógetsgwęh} \trs{she is having a gathering over there}, \trs{she is lifting something into a vertical position}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{segé:tsgoh} \trs{you raise something to a vertical position}

\lexicalunitbracket{gowanahd, gowanęhd} \trs{enlarge something, make something big}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gagowanáhtaˀ} \trs{it makes things big}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ęsehsgo̱haowá:neht} \trs{branch it out} (i.e. add particles, etc. to “dress up” speech)

\lexicalunitbracket{gri} \trs{wrinkle}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gegrihs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahsé:gri:k} \trs{you wrinkled, fan-folded it, you made it smaller, shrank it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dahsé:gri:k} \trs{wrinkle, fan-fold!}

\lexicalunitbracket{gw} \trs{gather, pick, get}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hegé:gwahs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{haˀhá:goˀ} \trs{he went and got it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agé:gwęh} \trs{how much I have obtained or acquired}

\lexicalunitbracket{gwah} \trs{go after}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{aˀǫdęnaˀtragwáhaˀ} \trs{she went after groceries}

\lexicalunitbracket{gwatw} \trs{hem}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhségwatoˀ} \trs{you will hem}

{\stative} \cayuga{degágwatwęh} \trs{hem}

\lexicalunitbracket{+gweg} \trs{close something}

{\habitual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ǫgyáˀdagwe:s} \trs{she gets bound up, constipated}

{\punctual}, with \textsc{srf+inc n} \cayuga{dęsátga̱hgwe:k} \trs{you will close your eyes}

{\stative}, with \textsc{srf+inc n} \cayuga{gogyaˀdagwé:gǫh} \trs{she is constipated}


\lexicalunitbracket{gweni, gweny} \trs{able to do something, succeed, win}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gegwé:nyeˀs}, \cayuga{gegwé:nyǫhs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęha:gwé:niˀ} \trs{he can do it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agégwenyǫ:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\subsubsection*{H-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}

\textsc{imp}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{segǫˀdró:we:k} \trs{you put the pillowcase on}

\lexicalunitbracket{hr} \trs{put, place}

{\habitual} \cayuga{kré:haˀ} \trs{I am setting (it on something)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhshręˀ} \trs{you will set it or place it on something}

{\stative} \cayuga{hewá:kre:ˀ} \trs{I put, placed it over there}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{itręh} \trs{you place it!}

\lexicalunitbracket{hręd} \trs{lead}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęháhę:t} \trs{he will lead}

{\stative} \cayuga{hahę́:dǫ:} \trs{he is the front, leader}

\lexicalunitbracket{hręˀda:} \trs{burn something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{krę́ˀda:s} \trs{I (always) burn something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsrę́ˀda:ˀ} \trs{you will burn something}

{\stative} \cayuga{akrę́ˀda:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{hreg} \trs{push}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hekre:s} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hękre:k} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{hewa:kré:gǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{hren, hre:} \trs{cut something with a knife}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ękre:ˀ} \trs{I will cut it}

{\stative} \cayuga{akré:nęh} \trs{I did cut it}

\lexicalunitbracket{hrenahnǫ} \trs{cut something up, shave with a knife}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsréna̱hnǫ:ˀ} \trs{you will shave (with a draw knife)}

\lexicalunitbracket{hretgęh} \trs{wreck something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsré:tgęh} \trs{you will wreck it}

\lexicalunitbracket{hretgęhd} \trs{damage something, ruin something, wrech something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhshé:tgęht} \trs{you will damage, ruin, wreck something}

{\stative} \cayuga{ga̱hétgę̱hdǫh} \trs{it is ruined, wrecked (by someone)}

\lexicalunitbracket{hriˀ, hiˀ} \trs{break up}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgáhiˀ} \trs{it will break (into small pieces)}

{\stative} \cayuga{deyóhiˀǫh} \trs{it is broken}

{\stative} \cayuga{hewákri̱hǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{degahehdáhihdǫh} \trs{land that is disced or worked}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dehsriht} \trs{grind!}


\lexicalunitbracket{hrǫhwę} \trs{bar something, put up a barrier}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsrǫ́hwęˀ} \trs{you will bar something, put up a barrier}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{agataháhsa:ˀ} \trs{I finished a road}


\lexicalunitbracket{hsadę} with \stem{{\cislocative}} and \textsc{p} \cayuga{prefix, means} \trs{mount a horse, come by horseback}, with \textsc{int} \cayuga{prefix, means} \trs{carry on one’s back}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgyago̱hsá:dęˀ} \trs{she will come by horseback}

\subsubsection*{I-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}



\lexicalunitbracket{i, ę} \trs{say}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀá:gęˀ} \trs{she did say}

{\stative} \cayuga{á:gę:} \trs{(that’s what) I did say}

Also see the full paradigm on page \pageref{figtab:1:say}.

\lexicalunitbracket{i:, ę:, e:} \trs{think, hope, want}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ihe:} \trs{he wants, thinks}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ehswe:ˀ} \trs{you all thought}

Also see the full paradigm on page \pageref{figtab:1:wantthink}.

\lexicalunitbracket{idagraˀ} \trs{fall down}

{\habitual} \cayuga{edá:graˀs} \trs{she is forever falling (i.e. an old person)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęyédagraˀ} \trs{she will fall down}

{\stative} \cayuga{agidagráˀǫh} \trs{I have fallen}

\lexicalunitbracket{idǫhgwahswahd} \trs{extinguish a flame, dim the lights}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsidǫ̱hgwáhstwaht} \trs{you will dim the lights}

{\stative} \cayuga{gędǫhgwa̱hstwáhdǫh} \trs{the flame is turned down}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdre} \trs{drag something, ride along in a vehicle, drive}

{\habitual} \cayuga{ǫkníˀdreˀ} \trs{we two are riding along in (something)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agéˀdre:ˀ} \trs{I dragged it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agéˀdrǫ:} \trs{I am dragging, I dragged}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desáˀdre:} \trs{drive over here}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdrehd} \trs{move oneself}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gadréhtaˀ} \trs{it moves itself, it rides}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdrǫd} \trs{live, dwell, be at home, reside, be placed, be situated}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsniˀdrǫ́:daˀk} \trs{you two will stay home}

\lexicalunitbracket{iˀdrǫdaˀ} \trs{land}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degęˀdrǫ́:daˀs} \trs{it lands there all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgęˀdrǫ́:daˀ} \trs{it will land}

{\stative} \cayuga{de̱hoˀdrǫdáˀǫh} \trs{he has landed}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihey, ihe:} \trs{die}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hęhé:yǫhs} \trs{he is dying}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgíhe:ˀ} \trs{I will die}

{\stative} \cayuga{awe:tˀá:ˀ agihé:yǫ:} \trs{I am pretending I am dead} \cayuga{awe:tˀá:ˀ} \trs{it is pretend}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihnagęˀdowę} \trs{put a patch on}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gi̱hnagęˀdówe̱haˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgihnagęˀdó:węˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agihnagę́ˀdo:ˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agihnanę́dakdǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihsag} \trs{seek, look for}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gi̱hsa:s} \trs{I am looking for it}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgíhsa:k} \trs{I will seek or look for it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agíhsagǫh} \trs{I am looking for it}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihsag} \trs{look for a mate}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{dedwáde̱hsa:s} \trs{we are looking for mates}

\lexicalunitbracket{ihsdęhd, sdęhd} \trs{scale fish}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęséhsdęht} \trs{you will take the scales off (the fish)}

\lexicalunitbracket{+iyaˀg} \trs{cut, break, cross something}

\subsubsection*{J-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{jagǫ} \trs{persevere, try hard}

\subsubsection*{K-stem, three-aspect, personal, changing from \textsc{a}- to \textsc{p}-series}
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{k} \trs{put together}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degé:kahs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgé:kaˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{degáekęh} \trs{twin girls, twin boy and girl}

\lexicalunitbracket{kahǫ} \trs{assemble, put together, match up}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhséka̱hǫˀ} \trs{you will assemble, put together, match or pair things up (puzzle pieces, socks)}

{\stative}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{deyonigyohgwakáhǫˀ} \trs{division of many organizations, i.e. Boy Scouts, Lions}

\lexicalunitbracket{kahsi} \trs{share, divide}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degékahsǫhs} \trs{I divide it}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsékahsiˀ} \trs{you will share, divide}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewagekáhsǫ:} \trs{I have taken one object apart}

\lexicalunitbracket{kahsǫgw} \trs{divide something into parts}, with \stem{({\dualic})}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsekahsǫ́:goˀ} \trs{you will divide it into parts}

{\stative} \cayuga{hoihwakáhsǫgweh} \trs{he has divided into parts or duties}

\lexicalunitbracket{kahsǫgwahǫ} \trs{divide into categories}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęsekahsǫ́gwa̱hǫˀ} \trs{you will divide them (several objects) up into categories}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{desekahsǫ́gwa̱hǫ:} \trs{you divide them (several objects) up into categories}

\lexicalunitbracket{kdaˀe} \trs{shell something}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dehsékda̱ˀe:k} \trs{shell (them)! hit the shell!}

\lexicalunitbracket{kdǫ} \trs{examine, look closely at, try (e.g., by tasting)}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hadíkdǫ̱haˀ} \trs{they examine it}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agé:kdǫ:ˀ} \trs{I did look closely at it}, \trs{I have examined it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agé:kdǫˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sekdǫ:} \trs{examine it!}

\lexicalunitbracket{kdǫnyǫ} \trs{examine fully}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsékdǫnyǫˀ} \trs{you will fully examine it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dwakdǫ́:nyǫ:} \trs{let’s examine}

\lexicalunitbracket{kdotsy} \trs{shell something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsékdotsih} \trs{you will shell (eggs, coconuts, etc.)}

\lexicalunitbracket{kǫni} \trs{cook something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gakǫ́:nihs} \trs{it cooks}

{\punctual} \cayuga{age:kǫ́:niˀ} \trs{I cooked a meal}

{\stative} \cayuga{gokǫ́:ni:} \trs{she is cooking}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sekǫ́:nih} \trs{cook}

\lexicalunitbracket{ksohaihǫ} \trs{go and wash dishes}

{\habitual} \cayuga{geksoháihǫh} \trs{I am washing dishes}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{seksoháihǫ:} \trs{wash the dishes}

\lexicalunitbracket{kwędaˀ} \trs{finish eating}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęga:kwę́:daˀ} \trs{it is going to finish eating}

{\stative} \cayuga{agekwędáˀǫh} \trs{I have finished eating}

\end{multicols}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫhwęjahsgęnh} \trs{fight over land}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{haǫhwęjáhsgenhahs} \trs{land researcher} (literally, \trs{he fights for land})

{\stative} \cayuga{saǫhwęjáhsgęnhęh} \trs{you are fighting over the land right now}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫhwęjahsnyeˀ} \trs{conserve land}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{deyǫkiyǫhwęjáhsnyeˀ} \trs{they look after our lands (title, office)}

\lexicalunitbracket{oˀjiyeˀg} \trs{suck, absorb}

{\habitual} \cayuga{goˀjíyeˀs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgoˀjí:ye:k} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agoˀjiyé:gǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{oˀjiyǫ} \trs{suck, absorb}

{\habitual} \cayuga{goˀjí:yǫhs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgoˀjí:yǫ:ˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agoˀjí:yǫˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{oˀkdę, oˀkdani} \trs{finish something}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hegóˀktaˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hęgóˀkdęˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫˀneg} \trs{remove something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gǫˀnéhs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgǫ́ˀne:k} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agǫˀné:gǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫˀn.eg} \trs{take away, subtract}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{tsǫˀnehs} \trs{you subtract, take away all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ętsǫ́ˀne:k} \trs{you will subtract}

{\stative} \cayuga{disǫ́ˀnǫ:} \trs{you have taken away}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{dahsǫ́ˀne:k} \trs{subtract!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫˀneksǫ} \trs{remove several things}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{sǫ̱ˀné:ksǫ:} \trs{you remove several things}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫnęhd} \trs{swallow}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hegǫ́nę̱htaˀ} \trs{I swallow}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hęgǫ́:nęht} \trs{I will swallow}

{\stative} \cayuga{hewagǫnę́hdǫh} \trs{I have swallowed}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{haˀsǫ́:nęht} \trs{you swallow!}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫnęhtge:} \trs{gulp}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{haˀgǫ́nę̱htge:} \trs{I took a big swallow (gulp)}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫni, ǫny} \trs{make, earn}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gǫ́:nih, gǫ́:nihs} \trs{I make, earn}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agǫ́:niˀ} \trs{I did make, earn}

{\stative} \cayuga{agǫ́:ni:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{sǫ́:nih} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫni, ǫny} \trs{use in place of something else, replace}, with \stem{{\contrastive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{tigǫ́:nihs} \trs{I use something in place of (something else)}

\lexicalunitbracket{owę} \trs{split in two}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{degaihó:węhs} \trs{computer}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atgó:wę:ˀ} \trs{I split it open}

{\stative}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}} \cayuga{deyo:dó:węˀ} \trs{it is split (in two)}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{desó:wę:} \trs{halve it!}


\lexicalunitbracket{otsy} \trs{remove an outer covering, shell}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gotsǫhs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgó:tsiˀ} \trs{I will strip skin off}

{\stative} \cayuga{agó:tsǫ:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ęhsékdotsiˀ} \trs{you will shell} (eggs, coconuts, etc.)

\lexicalunitbracket{+oweksy} \trs{uncover something}

\textsc{punc, with inc n} \cayuga{ęhsnaˀsgowé:ksih} \trs{you will uncover the bed}

\end{multicols}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdahsrǫni, yaˀdahsrǫny} \trs{dress something up}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gayaˀda̱hsrǫ́:nih} \trs{it dresses it up}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdęˀ} \trs{fall into}  (person), with \stem{{\translocative}/{\cislocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hegyáˀdęˀs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhtsyáˀdęˀ} \trs{you will fall into it}

{\stative} \cayuga{hewagyaˀdę́ˀǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdodrǫhgwaǫ} \trs{twitch}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sayaˀdodrǫhgwáǫhaˀ} \trs{you are twitching (right now)}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdodrǫhgwaǫni} \trs{shiver}

{\habitual} \cayuga{sayaˀdodrǫhgwáǫnihsgǫ:} \trs{you are always shivering}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdowehd} \trs{think about, consider}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{deyeya̱ˀdówe̱htaˀ} \trs{she is a thinker (seer)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgyaˀdó:weht} \trs{I will think over}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewagya̱ˀdówe̱hdǫh} \trs{I have already thought about it}, \trs{I am thinking about it}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀdrę} \trs{put on top}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degyáˀdre̱haˀ}, \cayuga{degyaˀdré:haˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęgyáˀdręˀ} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{dewágyaˀse:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀg} \trs{cut}

{\habitual} \cayuga{igyaˀs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgyaˀk} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\stative} \cayuga{agyáˀgǫh} \citep{sasse_far_1998}




\lexicalunitbracket{yagę} \trs{go out}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gyá:gęˀs} \trs{I am going out}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyá:gęˀ} \trs{you will go out}

{\stative} \cayuga{heyoyagę́ˀǫh} \trs{that’s where it went out}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaˀgyenę} \trs{fall over, pass on, die}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahayagyé:nęˀ} \trs{he fell over} (refers to passing on)

\lexicalunitbracket{yahnǫ} \trs{touch, pick at, grope}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hehsyáhnǫhaˀ} \trs{you are picking at something} (i.e. your food), \trs{you are a groper}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hęhsyáhnǫ:ˀ} \trs{you will grope, touch, pick at}

{\stative} \cayuga{hehsyáhnǫh} \trs{you are touching here and there, groping}

\lexicalunitbracket{yaǫ} \trs{bead something}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{desyáǫhaˀ} \trs{you are beading}

{\stative} \cayuga{degáyaǫˀ} \trs{it is beaded}



\lexicalunitbracket{yę} \trs{set, put, place something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hayę́hęˀ} \trs{he puts, places it there (continuously)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyę:ˀ} \trs{you will put it there!}

{\stative} \cayuga{nigá:yęˀ} \trs{where it is at, where it is placed}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{iję:} \trs{you put it down}, \trs{leave it alone!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yę} \trs{put things side by side, lie side by side}, with \stem{{\coincident},{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{tsaˀdę́hsyę:ˀ} \trs{you will put, lay them side by side}

{\stative} \cayuga{tsaˀdégayęˀ} \trs{it is lying or setting side by side}

\lexicalunitbracket{yę} \trs{gamble, bet, play a game}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\stative} \cayuga{de̱ho:dí:yęˀ, deto:dí:yęˀ} \trs{they are gambling, betting}

\lexicalunitbracket{ye:, yę:} \trs{do}

{\habitual} \cayuga{nigyé:haˀ} \trs{I do}

{\punctual} \cayuga{nę́:gye:ˀ} \trs{I will do}

{\stative} \cayuga{nigyó:yę:} \trs{what it is doing}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{sgęnǫ:ˀǫ́h nęh tsye:} \trs{you take your time} \cayuga{sgęnǫ:ˀǫ́h} \trs{slowly} \cayuga{nęh} \trs{now}

\lexicalunitbracket{ye:, yę:} \trs{touch}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hehsyé:haˀ} \trs{you are a toucher}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hęhsye:ˀ} \trs{you will touch}

{\stative} \cayuga{hehsá:yę:} \trs{you did touch something}

\lexicalunitbracket{yeh} \trs{awake, wake up}

{\habitual} \cayuga{igyehs} \trs{I wake up (all the time)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyeh} \trs{you will wake up!}

{\stative} \cayuga{sá:ye:} \trs{you are awake}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{ijeh} \trs{wake up!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yędaˀ} \trs{become, acquire, obtain}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gayę́:daˀs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsa:yę́:daˀ} \trs{you will acquire, obtain}

{\stative} \cayuga{oyę́daˀǫ}h \citep{sasse_far_1998}


\lexicalunitbracket{yędei, yędi} \trs{know}

{\stative} \cayuga{dejidwayę́:di:} \trs{we all do not know any longer}

\lexicalunitbracket{yędr, yęs} \trs{skin something}, also see \stem{yęse} (next column)

{\habitual} \cayuga{gyędrǫhs} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgyę́:se:ˀ} \trs{I will skin}

{\stative} \cayuga{agyę́:drǫ:} \citep{sasse_far_1998}

\lexicalunitbracket{yęˀgwaˀe} \trs{tan something, smoke something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyę́ˀgwaˀe:k} \trs{you will smoke it} (meat, etc.), \trs{you will tan it}

\lexicalunitbracket{yęhętw, yęhęto} \trs{pull something}, with \stem{{\translocative}/{\cislocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ętgyę́hętoˀ} \trs{I will pull it}

\lexicalunitbracket{yehsd} \trs{mix together}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęsyehs} \trs{you will mix them all together}

{\stative}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{degahnegáye̱hsdǫh} \trs{water is mixed in it}

\textsc{imp}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}}  \cayuga{dehsnégayehs} \trs{dilute it with water!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yenaw, yenaǫ, yena:} \trs{catch, receive, accept, hold something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gyé:nahs, gyenáǫhs} \trs{I catch, receive, accept, hold it}

{\punctual} \cayuga{agyé:na:ˀ} \trs{I caught it}, \trs{I received it}

{\stative} \cayuga{agye:náǫ:, agyé:na:} \trs{I have caught it, received it}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{ję́:na:} \trs{you (s) catch it! (an animal, etc.)}

\lexicalunitbracket{yenaw, yenaǫ, yena:} \trs{grab something}, with \stem{{\cislocative}/{\translocative}} 

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{datsę́:na:} \trs{you grab it!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yenaw, yenaǫ, yena:} \trs{work together}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atadiyé:na:ˀ} \trs{they did it together (i.e. accomplices)}

\lexicalunitbracket{yenawaˀkǫ} \trs{work together, be complicit, be accomplices}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{degadiyenawáˀkǫˀ} \trs{they are accomplices}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dedwayenáwa̱ˀkǫ:} \trs{let’s work together}

\lexicalunitbracket{yęse} \trs{skin something}

{\habitual} \cayuga{syę́:sehs} \trs{you skin animals all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyę́:se:ˀ} \trs{you will skin it}

{\stative} \cayuga{sayę́:se:} \trs{you are skinning it right now}

\lexicalunitbracket{yętw, yęto} \trs{plant}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gyę́:twahs} \trs{I plant it}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ęknǫhsayę́:toˀ} \trs{I will plant onions}

{\stative} \cayuga{tęˀ dehóyętwęh} \trs{he did not plant}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{tęˀ taháyętoh} \trs{he will not plant}

\lexicalunitbracket{yętwagw, yętwago} \trs{harvest}

{\habitual} \cayuga{hayę́twagwahs} \trs{he is harvesting}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahayętwá:goˀ} \trs{he did harvest}

{\stative} \cayuga{hoyę́twagwęh} \trs{he harvested it}



\lexicalunitbracket{yidahsd} \trs{do right}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{de̱hsyí:dahs} \trs{you do things right}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫ} \trs{arrive}

{\habitual} \cayuga{é:yǫhs} \trs{she arrives (at the same time)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀé:yǫˀ} \trs{she arrived}

{\stative} \cayuga{gó:yǫ:} \trs{she has arrived}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫ} \trs{come in}, with \stem{{\cislocative}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{itgyǫhs} \trs{I come in (from the same place) all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{daga:dí:yǫˀ} \trs{they came in}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{dajǫh} \trs{come in!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫ} \trs{return, come back}, with \stem{{\repetitive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{shá:yǫˀ} \trs{he returned}

{\stative} \cayuga{shó:yǫ:} \trs{he returned}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫ} \trs{go in}, with \stem{{\translocative}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{haˀgyǫˀ} \trs{I went in}

{\stative} \cayuga{heho:dí:yǫ:} \trs{they arrived, they went in there}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫ} \trs{go back inside}, with \stem{{\translocative},{\repetitive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{hǫsahá:yǫˀ} \trs{he went back inside}, \trs{he arrived back there}

\textsc{imp} \cayuga{haˀjǫh, haˀsyǫh} \trs{go in, enter!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫˀd} \trs{bring something, score a goal}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahá:yǫˀt} \trs{he scored}, \trs{he brought it}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫˀd} \trs{bring something back}, with \stem{{\repetitive}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsgáeyǫˀt} \trs{they will bring it back}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫgyaˀd} \trs{laugh}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gyǫgyáˀtaˀ} \trs{I am really laughing}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyǫ́:gyaˀt} \trs{you will smile!}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫgyaˀtge:} \trs{guffaw}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęsyǫ́gya̱ˀtge:} \trs{you will laugh loudly, guffaw}

\lexicalunitbracket{yǫwadahgw} \trs{eviscerate something, gut something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsyǫwadáhgoˀ} \trs{you will gut something}


\end{multicols}



\subsubsection*{Three-aspect irregular verb \stem{i, e, ę, adǫh} \trs{say}}
Three-aspect irregular verb \stem{i, e, ę, adǫh} \trs{say} takes regular pronominal prefixes, but is otherwise irregular in that the meaning is conveyed by four separate stems: the stem \stem{iˀ} and \stem{ęˀ} in the punctual, \stem{ę:} in the stative, and \stem{adǫh} in the habitual. The complete paradigm is shown in \tabref{figtab:1:say}, p. \pageref{figtab:1:say}. All forms are from \citet{sasse_far_1998}.

%<\$img:say’;w= 350;ebook=50\%>
\begin{table}
\caption{Say\label{figtab:1:say}}
\begin{tabularx}{\textwidth}{XXX}
\lsptoprule
factual punctual & stative & habitual\\
\midrule
\cayuga{agíˀ} \trs{I said} & \cayuga{á:gę:} \trs{I have said} & \cayuga{ga:dǫh} \trs {I say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{á:kniˀ, aˀá:kniˀ} \trs{we two (not you) said} & \cayuga{ǫknę:} \trs{we two have said} & \cayuga{agyá:dǫh} \trs{we two say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{ekníˀ, etníˀ} \trs{you and I said}  & & \cayuga{gyá:dǫh} \trs{you and I say} \\\midrule
\cayuga{á:gwęˀ, aˀá:gwęˀ} \trs{we, not you, said} & \cayuga{ǫ́:gwę} \trs{we all have said} & \cayuga{agwá:dǫh} \trs{we, not you, say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{edwęˀ, etwęˀ} \trs{we and you said}  & & \cayuga{dwá:dǫh} \trs{we and you say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{asíˀ} \trs{you (one) said} & \cayuga{í:sę:} \trs{you (one) have said} & \cayuga{sá:dǫh} \trs{you (one) say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{esníˀ} \trs{you two said} & \cayuga{ihsnę:} \trs{you two have said} & \cayuga{já:dǫh} \trs{you two say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{eswęˀ}  \trs{you all said} & \cayuga{ihswę:} \trs{you all have said} & \cayuga{swá:dǫh} \trs{you all say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{ahęˀ} \trs{he said} & \cayuga{há:wę:} \trs{he has said} & \cayuga{há:dǫh} \trs{he says} \\\midrule
\cayuga{á:gęˀ, aˀá:gęˀ} \trs{she said} & \cayuga{gá:wę:} \trs{she has said} & \cayuga{ǫ́:dǫh} \trs{she, someone says}\\\midrule
\cayuga{awęˀ} \trs{it said} & \cayuga{á:wę:} \trs{it has said} & \cayuga{wá:dǫh} \trs{it is said}\\\midrule
\cayuga{ahę:niˀ} \trs{they (males) said} & \cayuga{hó:nę:} \trs{they (males) have said}  & \cayuga{hęná:dǫh} \trs{they (males) say} \\\midrule
\cayuga{agá:gęˀ} \trs{they (fe/males) said} & \cayuga{gó:nę:} \trs{they (fe/males) have said} & \cayuga{gaǫgadǫh} \trs{they (fe/males) say}\\\midrule
\cayuga{agę:niˀ} \trs{they (animals) said} & \cayuga{ó:nę:} \trs{they (animals) have said}  & \cayuga{gęná:dǫh} \trs{they (animals) say}\\
\lspbottomrule
\end{tabularx}
\end{table}

\subsubsection*{Three-aspect irregular verb \stem{i:, e:} \trs{want, think}}
The irregular paradigm for the verb meaning \trs{to want, think} is listed in \tabref{figtab:1:wantthink}, p. \pageref{figtab:1:wantthink}. All forms are from \citet{sasse_far_1998}.

\begin{table}[t]
\caption{Want, think}
\label{figtab:1:wantthink}
\tiny{
\begin{tabularx}{\textwidth}{XXXXX}
\lsptoprule
stative & stative past & factual punctual & indefinite punctual & future punctual\\
\midrule
í:wi:

\trs{I want, think} & \cayuga{gehéhk}

\trs{I was thinking} & \cayuga{ahí:ˀ}

\trs{I wanted, thought} & \cayuga{ǫ́:wi:ˀ}
\trs{I should want, think} & \cayuga{ęhi:ˀ}

\trs{I will want, think}\\

\trs{we two (not you) want, think} & \cayuga{aknéhehk}

\trs{you and I want, think} & \cayuga{knehehk}

\trs{you (s) will want, think}\\

\trs{you two were thinking} & \cayuga{esne:ˀ}

\trs{you two wanted, thought} & \cayuga{áesne:ˀ}
\trs{you two should want, think} & \cayuga{ęhsne:ˀ}

\trs{you two will want, think}\\
\midrule 
ihswé:

\trs{you all want, think} & \cayuga{swehehk}

\trs{you all were thinking} & \cayuga{eswe:ˀ}

\trs{you all wanted, thought} & \cayuga{áeswe:ˀ}

\trs{you all should want, think} & \cayuga{ęhswe:ˀ}

\trs{you all will want, think}\\
\midrule 
ihé:

\trs{he wants, thinks} & \cayuga{hehehk}

\trs{he wants, thinks} & \cayuga{ahe:ˀ}

\trs{he wanted, thought} & \cayuga{á:he:ˀ}

\trs{he should want, think} & \cayuga{ęhe:ˀ}

\trs{he will want, think}\\
\midrule 
í:yę:

\trs{she wants, thinks} & \cayuga{ęhehk}

\trs{she wanted, thought} & \cayuga{á:yę:ˀ}

\trs{it will want, think}\\

hę́:ne:

\trs{they (males) want, think} & \cayuga{hęnéhehk}

\trs{they (males) wanted, thought} & \cayuga{a:hę́:ne:ˀ}

\trs{they (males) should want, think} & \cayuga{ęhę́:ne:ˀ}

\trs{they (males) will want, think}\\
\midrule 
gáę

\trs{they (females or mixed group) want, think} & \cayuga{gáęhk}

\trs{they (females or mixed group) were thinking} & \cayuga{agáęˀ}

\trs{they (females or mixed group) wanted, thought} & \cayuga{á:gaęˀ}

\trs{they (females or mixed group) should want, think} & \cayuga{ęgáęˀ}

\trs{they (females or mixed group) will want, think}\\
\midrule 
gę́:ne:

\trs{they (animals) want, think} & \cayuga{gęnéhehk}

\trs{they (animals) were thinking} & \cayuga{agę́:ne:ˀ}

\trs{they (animals) wanted, thought} & \cayuga{a:gę́:ne:ˀ}

\trs{they (animals) should want, think} & \cayuga{ęgę́:ne:ˀ}

\trs{they (animals) will want, think}\\
\lspbottomrule
\end{tabularx}}
\end{table}

\subsection{Three-aspect verbs taking only \textsc{p}-series personal prefixes }
\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{adadę} \trs{end up with something, remain, have leftovers, be leftover}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgadadę:ˀ} \trs{I remained}, \trs{I was left over}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgadadę:ˀs} \trs{I ended up with it (i.e. leftovers)}

\lexicalunitbracket{adaˀi:s} \trs{have intercourse, mate}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\stative} \cayuga{onadaˀí:sęh} \trs{they are mating}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{sadáˀi:s} \trs{you have intercourse}


\lexicalunitbracket{adedręhdatgidę, adedręhdatgidani} \trs{have nightmares, bad dreams}, with \stem{{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{agadedręhdatgidaníhsgę̱hę:ˀ} \trs{I used to have bad dreams}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgadedręhdatgí:dęˀ} \trs{I had a bad dream}

\lexicalunitbracket{adęhǫgai, adęhǫgany} \trs{suffer}, with \stem{{\dualic},{\semireflexive}}

{\habitual} \cayuga{desadęhǫ́gais} \trs{you suffer all the time}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsadęhǫ́gaiˀ} \trs{you will suffer}

{\stative} \cayuga{dęsadęhǫ́ganyęh} \trs{you are suffering right now}

{\stative} \cayuga{oˀnigǫ̱hsá:dǫhk} \trs{it is lonesome, mournful}

\lexicalunitbracket{nihsgw} \trs{be late}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwáknihsgoˀ} \trs{I will be late}

{\stative} \cayuga{aknihsgo̱ˀǫ́hǫgyeˀ} \trs{I am arriving late}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫ} \trs{unable}

{\habitual} \cayuga{aknǫ́haˀ} \trs{I am unable}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwá:knǫ:ˀ} \trs{I will be unable}

{\stative} \cayuga{honǫ́ˀǫh} \trs{he is unable}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫdanhaˀ} \trs{be found guilty}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahonǫdá:nhaˀ} \trs{he was found guilty}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnodra} \trs{have skin sores, be infected}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęhsaˀno:dráˀ sehsóhgwa̱ˀgeh} \trs{you will have sores on your lips}

{\stative} \cayuga{oˀnó:draˀ} \trs{it is infected}, \trs{an infection}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnodrahsd} \trs{have, get a skin infection, rash, allergic reaction}

{\habitual} \cayuga{go̱ˀnó:drahs} \trs{she has open, weeping sores}

{\punctual} \cayuga{aˀago̱ˀnó:drahs} \trs{she got chicken pox, a skin infection, allergic reactions}, \trs{she became infected}

{\stative} \cayuga{sa̱ˀnódra̱hsdǫh} \trs{it has given you an infection, an allergic reaction}, \trs{you have already had an allergic reaction}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫhaged} \trs{put one’s head down}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęhsanǫ̱há:ge:t} \trs{you will put your head down}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫhnyaˀg} \trs{be, get hurt}

{\habitual} \cayuga{aknǫ́hnyaˀs} \trs{I hurt}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwáknǫ̱hyaˀk} \trs{I will get hurt}

{\stative} \cayuga{honǫ́hnya̱ˀgǫh} \trs{he is hurt}

\lexicalunitbracket{nǫˀs} \trs{tire of something, get sick of something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫˀknǫˀs} \trs{I am sick of it, bored, fed up}, \trs{I got sick of it}



\lexicalunitbracket{nyag} \trs{be married}

{\habitual} \cayuga{agé:nya:s} \trs{I am getting married right now}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwágenya:k} \trs{I will be married}

{\stative} \cayuga{agényagǫh} \trs{I am married}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀnyagę} \trs{pass wind, fart}

{\habitual} \cayuga{agóˀnyagęˀs} \trs{she passing wind, farting}


\lexicalunitbracket{nyaˀgw, nyaˀgo} \trs{vomit}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgénya̱ˀgoˀ} \trs{I vomited}

{\stative} \cayuga{agenya̱ˀgwáhǫh} \trs{I am vomiting (right now)}

\lexicalunitbracket{oˀgwad} \trs{dig}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫˀwesahs} \trs{have a good time}

{\habitual} \cayuga{agǫ́ˀweshahs} \trs{I am having a good time, enjoying something}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫˀwesę, ǫˀwesgwani} \trs{enjoy oneself}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwagǫ̱ˀwé:sęˀ} \trs{I will enjoy myself}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫwihshęˀǫh} \trs{pant, be short of breath}

{\stative} \cayuga{gaǫwi̱hshę́ˀǫh} \trs{she is panting}

\lexicalunitbracket{ra:dog} \trs{blister one’s heel}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgrá:do:k} \trs{I blistered my heel}

\lexicalunitbracket{rihwaędaˀ} \trs{decide}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{atoihwáędaˀs} \trs{he came to a decision or conclusion}

\textsc{imper} \cayuga{dehsaihwáędaˀs} \trs{you decide}

\lexicalunitbracket{sw, sho} \trs{smell (involuntarily)}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęwágeshoˀ} \trs{I will smell it (unintentionally)}

with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{go̱heyǫdá:swahs} \trs{she smells a dead body}

\lexicalunitbracket{ˀtsǫhsd} \trs{sneeze}, with \stem{{\dualic}}

{\punctual} \cayuga{dęsáˀtsǫhs} \trs{you will sneeze}

\lexicalunitbracket{węnaˀd} \trs{give up}

{\punctual} \cayuga{esa:wę́:naˀt} \trs{you gave up}

\lexicalunitbracket{węnaˀehsd} \trs{stutter}

\lexicalunitbracket{wiyageheyaˀs} \trs{die} (said of a baby)

{\punctual} \cayuga{ǫgyáˀda̱hshęˀ} \trs{I was late}

{\habitual} \cayuga{gǫyǫhwadá:nih} \trs{I am showing you something}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ęgǫ́hwadęˀ} \trs{I will charge}

{\stative} \cayuga{agǫhwadá:nih} \trs{it has shown me something}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫni, ǫny} \trs{make, earn for someone}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ashagonǫhsǫ́:niˀ} \trs{he built a house for her}

\lexicalunitbracket{ǫnyę} \trs{make for someone}

{\punctual}, with \stem{\textsc{inc n}} \cayuga{ahǫwadinǫ̱hsǫ́:nyęˀ} \trs{they built him a house}


\end{multicols}

\subsubsection*{R, S-stem, three-aspect, interactive}

\begin{multicols}{2}


\lexicalunitbracket{ręnanhodǫgw} \trs{take over a song from someone}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahǫwaęnanho:dǫ́goˀ} \trs{he took over the song}

\lexicalunitbracket{rihǫd} \trs{appoint someone, delegate someone}

{\punctual} \cayuga{ahǫwaihǫ́:dęˀ} \trs{they delegated him a duty}

{\stative} \cayuga{shǫgwáihǫ:t} \trs{he has appointed us}
